--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
```python
from pathlib import Path

md = &quot;&quot;&quot;# Hub Suite (Compare · Stream · Navigator · Broker) — R4 Product &amp; Technical Design Document
*Version:* 0.9 (Draft)  
*Date:* 2026-01-01  
*Scope:* Roadmap R4 (Connectors/Marketplace/Bridges, MegaCatalog Navigation, AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label)  
*Context:* R1–R3 already cover Hub shell, canonical data model, ingestion basics, search+facets, Stream events, Compare scoring, Orders/Claims, Trust baseline, tech foundation.

---

## 0) Executive summary
You are building a **compact “office-suite style” hub** for commerce &amp; services information:
- **Compare App** — compare offers/services/insurances/travel options with explainable ranking.
- **Stream App** — “news conference” feed: clustered events, price changes, releases, risks, daily/weekly briefs.
- **Navigator App** — solves mega-catalog pain (Temu/Ali): better search, facets, normalization, dedup, guided narrowing.
- **Broker App** — brokerage layer: affiliate/deeplinks, optional order orchestration, service fulfillment routing.

**R4 adds three platform upgrades:**
1) **Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges** (n8n/Node-RED style, but curated and reliable).  
2) **MegaCatalog Navigation** (normalization + entity resolution + hybrid semantic search; optional visual search).  
3) **AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label** (assistant on top; explainability-first; multi-tenant packaging).

---

## 1) Goals and non-goals

### 1.1 Goals (R4)
- Make data acquisition/partners scalable via **connectors** with strict contracts.
- Turn poor mega-catalog experiences into a differentiator: **you find the right item faster**.
- Add AI features that are **safe and evidence-based**: no hallucinated claims, always linked to facts.
- Enable **B2B packaging** (white-label) without creating a fragile mega-monolith.

### 1.2 Non-goals (R4)
- Compete with full Make.com / Zapier ecosystem. Instead: **20–50 curated bridges**.
- “General web crawler” at scale like a search engine. Instead: **source-configured ingestion**.
- Fully automated purchase/payment across all partners. Use **pluggable checkout** and “action connectors”.

---

## 2) Product structure: “Office suite” inside one Hub

### 2.1 Apps (modules) and responsibilities
1) **Compare App**
   - Offer table, sorting, filters, watchlists
   - Scoring + explain panel
   - Export (CSV), share internal links

2) **Stream App**
   - Event clustering (“conference”), timelines
   - Lenses: News, Price, Risk, Release, Reviews
   - Daily/weekly/monthly briefs

3) **Navigator App**
   - Hybrid search + facets
   - Guided narrowing (category wizards)
   - Dedup, canonical entities, normalization
   - “Bad search mode”: typo tolerance, synonym mapping

4) **Broker App**
   - Deeplink/affiliate tracking
   - Optional: order creation + fulfillment routing + claims

5) **Admin/Moderation App**
   - Source Manager, connector install/update
   - Merge queue, risk moderation, compatibility moderation
   - Data quality dashboards

### 2.2 Shared platform services (cross-app)
- **Shared Core Data Model** (Entity/Offer/Event/Review/Order/Claim/Supplier/SourceConfig)
- **Event Bus** (publish/subscribe + idempotency)
- **Search + Facet Index**
- **Trust/Risk Engine**
- **Connector Runtime + Registry**
- **Analytics + Observability**

---

## 3) Architecture blueprint (R4)

### 3.1 Layers (4-level “tree/branch” model)
- **L0 — Runtime/Host:** Android app + (optional) server-mode.
- **L1 — Hub Core:** data model, event bus, indexing, permissions, audit.
- **L2 — Apps:** Compare/Stream/Navigator/Broker/Admin.
- **L3 — Connectors + Bridges:** ingestion/action plugins + external automations.

### 3.2 Data flow (high level)
1) SourceConfig schedules import → Connector fetches data  
2) Connector normalizes → upserts canonical entities/offers/events  
3) Event Bus emits domain events  
4) Indexers update search/facets + graph relations  
5) Apps render views; rules/AI add explanations/summaries  
6) Action connectors handle outbound (affiliate links, webhooks, exports)

### 3.3 Security baseline for R4 platformization
- **Capability sandbox** for connectors:
  - network allowlist, storage constraints, no arbitrary file access
  - explicit PII access permission (default deny)
- **Signed connector packages** + version pinning
- **Contract tests** required to publish a connector to registry
- **Webhook security**: signatures, nonces, replay protection

---

## 4) R4-1: Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges

### 4.1 Connector types
**Ingestion connectors (input):**
- RSS/Atom; Merchant feeds (CSV/TSV/XML); price feeds; review feeds; release notes feeds; partner APIs.

**Action connectors (output):**
- Deeplink generators; outbound webhook; export to CSV/PDF; order routing; partner status updates.

### 4.2 Connector SDK v2 (what’s inside)
- lifecycle: `init → validateConfig → run → emit`
- standard utilities:
  - rate limiting, retries/backoff, ETag caching, timeouts/circuit breaker
  - schema validation on input/output
  - structured logging + ingestion tracing spans
- test harness:
  - golden tests, fuzz tests, contract tests
- governance:
  - versioning, deprecation, migration notes

### 4.3 Internal Marketplace (Registry)
- searchable catalog (by category, source-type, rating, stability)
- install/update/rollback
- compatibility matrix (Hub version ↔ connector version)
- health and reliability score per connector
- license + SBOM + signature metadata

### 4.4 Bridges pack (curated automation)
**Goal:** give “Make-like power” without complexity.
- 10–20 “recipes” v1 (e.g., send Telegram digest, sync to Google Sheets, create Trello card on risk event)
- strict contracts, templates, and observability
- sandbox replay tool for webhooks

### 4.5 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** scalable ecosystem, faster partner onboarding, modular growth.  
**Cons:** requires governance; without contracts you get breakage &amp; chaos.

---

## 5) R4-2: MegaCatalog Navigation (Temu/Ali painkiller)

### 5.1 Key differentiator
A mega-catalog fails when:
- attributes are messy or missing,
- duplicates dominate results,
- filters are weak,
- search doesn’t understand intent.

**Your differentiator:** “Navigator App” builds a *canonical, normalized, deduped* view with hybrid search and guided narrowing.

### 5.2 Subsystems
1) **Normalization engine**
   - units (cm/in, kg/lb), currencies, shipping time formats
   - brand/model dictionaries
   - package/variants (color/storage/bundle)

2) **Entity resolution 2.0**
   - candidate generation (text + attributes + price history + seller)
   - safe merge + rollback
   - graph relations: variant-of, clone-of, alternative, compatible

3) **Hybrid search**
   - lexical (exact for model/MPN/SKU)
   - semantic (meaning, synonyms, typos)
   - facets + explain why-result

4) **Guided search v2**
   - category scripts (questions → facets)
   - store preferences; offer quick toggles

5) **Catalog quality analytics**
   - empty result rate, reformulations, abandon rate
   - attribute completeness, dup ratio
   - “top pain categories” report

6) **(Optional) Visual search**
   - image embeddings for “find similar”
   - risk: compute cost and dataset needs; keep optional behind flag

### 5.3 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** very strong UX, clear UTP vs existing portals.  
**Cons:** more data work; needs careful evaluation to avoid wrong merges.

---

## 6) R4-3: AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label

### 6.1 AI principles (must-have)
- **Evidence-first:** every statement links to hub facts (fields/events/sources).
- **No autonomous buying:** AI suggests; core rules execute.
- **Conservative mode:** if confidence low, ask questions or show alternatives.

### 6.2 Copilot modes
1) **Intent → Query/Facets** (turn natural language into filters)
2) **Explain ranking** (why this offer is top)
3) **Summaries** (events weekly, reviews themes, risk digest)
4) **Action coach** (next best action)
5) **Personalization** (preferences, risk tolerance)
6) **White-label** (tenant config, feature flags, branding)

### 6.3 Personalization and privacy
- opt-in telemetry
- user can view/edit/delete stored preferences
- PII minimization: store preferences, not identities; keep exports safe

### 6.4 White-label packaging
- tenant configs (modules enabled, default lenses, partner lists)
- theme/branding
- rule packs per tenant
- multi-tenant isolation (server-mode) or “profiles” (local mode)

---

## 7) Metrics and success criteria

### 7.1 MegaCatalog success metrics
- ↓ empty-result rate
- ↓ average time-to-first-good-result
- ↓ reformulation count
- ↓ duplicate ratio in top-20 results
- ↑ conversion proxy: clicks to trusted offers / saved shortlist

### 7.2 Stream success metrics
- ↑ daily brief opens
- ↓ notification spam (dedup window hit rate)
- ↑ follow/subscription retention

### 7.3 Connectors platform metrics
- connector install success rate
- ingestion failure rate p95
- MTTR for connector breakage
- registry rollback usage

### 7.4 AI quality &amp; safety metrics
- % answers with evidence links
- hallucination incidents (should be ~0)
- user trust rating per answer (thumbs)
- “AI asked clarifying questions” rate when low confidence

---

## 8) Risks and mitigations
- **Wrong merges** → require moderation queue, rollback, confidence threshold.
- **Connector breakage** (partner changes format) → contract tests + canary + rollback.
- **AI over-claims** → evidence gating + conservative mode + policy templates.
- **Privacy** → PII inventory, opt-in, masking in exports, strict RBAC.
- **Scope creep** → keep curated bridges; avoid “100k integrations” trap.

---

## 9) Roadmap snapshot
- **R4.0:** Connector SDK v2 + Registry v1 + curated Bridges v1 + Hybrid search baseline
- **R4.1:** Normalization &amp; Entity Resolution 2.0 + Guided search v2 + Catalog QA dashboards
- **R4.2:** AI Copilot (intent + summaries) + Personalization controls + White-label beta
- **R4.3:** Optional visual search, advanced risk + multi-tenant hardening

---

## 10) Open questions (to finalize before implementation)
1) Server-mode required from day 1, or “local-first” only with optional server later?
2) Which 10–20 bridges are “must-have” for MVP (Telegram, Sheets, Email, etc.)?
3) Which mega-catalog categories first (electronics? tools? travel offers? insurance tariffs?)?
4) What is the acceptable false-merge rate (target threshold) before auto-merge is allowed?

---

## Appendix A — Terminology
- **Entity:** canonical product/service item
- **Offer:** concrete proposal (price, seller, delivery)
- **Event:** clustered news/price/release/risk update
- **Review:** user review items with topics
- **Trust/Risk:** signals and scores
- **Connector:** plugin for ingest/action
- **Bridge:** curated automation integration
&quot;&quot;&quot;

headers = [&quot;External ID&quot;,&quot;Issue Type&quot;,&quot;Summary&quot;,&quot;Description&quot;,&quot;Acceptance Criteria&quot;,&quot;Priority&quot;,&quot;Story Points&quot;,&quot;Epic Name&quot;,&quot;Epic Link&quot;,&quot;Dependencies&quot;,&quot;Release&quot;,&quot;Estimate T-Shirt&quot;]
rows = [&quot;,&quot;.join([f&quot;\&quot;{h}\&quot;&quot; for h in headers])]

def add_row(ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt):
    row = [ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, str(sp), epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt]
    rows.append(&quot;,&quot;.join([f&quot;\&quot;{str(x).replace(&#x27;\&quot;&#x27;,&#x27;\&quot;\&quot;&#x27;)}\&quot;&quot; for x in row]))

# Epics
```

--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
from pathlib import Path

md = &quot;&quot;&quot;# Hub Suite (Compare · Stream · Navigator · Broker) — R4 Product &amp; Technical Design Document
*Version:* 0.9 (Draft)  
*Date:* 2026-01-01  
*Scope:* Roadmap R4 (Connectors/Marketplace/Bridges, MegaCatalog Navigation, AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label)  
*Context:* R1–R3 already cover Hub shell, canonical data model, ingestion basics, search+facets, Stream events, Compare scoring, Orders/Claims, Trust baseline, tech foundation.

---

## 0) Executive summary
You are building a **compact “office-suite style” hub** for commerce &amp; services information:
- **Compare App** — compare offers/services/insurances/travel options with explainable ranking.
- **Stream App** — “news conference” feed: clustered events, price changes, releases, risks, daily/weekly briefs.
- **Navigator App** — solves mega-catalog pain (Temu/Ali): better search, facets, normalization, dedup, guided narrowing.
- **Broker App** — brokerage layer: affiliate/deeplinks, optional order orchestration, service fulfillment routing.

**R4 adds three platform upgrades:**
1) **Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges** (n8n/Node-RED style, but curated and reliable).  
2) **MegaCatalog Navigation** (normalization + entity resolution + hybrid semantic search; optional visual search).  
3) **AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label** (assistant on top; explainability-first; multi-tenant packaging).

---

## 1) Goals and non-goals

### 1.1 Goals (R4)
- Make data acquisition/partners scalable via **connectors** with strict contracts.
- Turn poor mega-catalog experiences into a differentiator: **you find the right item faster**.
- Add AI features that are **safe and evidence-based**: no hallucinated claims, always linked to facts.
- Enable **B2B packaging** (white-label) without creating a fragile mega-monolith.

### 1.2 Non-goals (R4)
- Compete with full Make.com / Zapier ecosystem. Instead: **20–50 curated bridges**.
- “General web crawler” at scale like a search engine. Instead: **source-configured ingestion**.
- Fully automated purchase/payment across all partners. Use **pluggable checkout** and “action connectors”.

---

## 2) Product structure: “Office suite” inside one Hub

### 2.1 Apps (modules) and responsibilities
1) **Compare App**
   - Offer table, sorting, filters, watchlists
   - Scoring + explain panel
   - Export (CSV), share internal links

2) **Stream App**
   - Event clustering (“conference”), timelines
   - Lenses: News, Price, Risk, Release, Reviews
   - Daily/weekly/monthly briefs

3) **Navigator App**
   - Hybrid search + facets
   - Guided narrowing (category wizards)
   - Dedup, canonical entities, normalization
   - “Bad search mode”: typo tolerance, synonym mapping

4) **Broker App**
   - Deeplink/affiliate tracking
   - Optional: order creation + fulfillment routing + claims

5) **Admin/Moderation App**
   - Source Manager, connector install/update
   - Merge queue, risk moderation, compatibility moderation
   - Data quality dashboards

### 2.2 Shared platform services (cross-app)
- **Shared Core Data Model** (Entity/Offer/Event/Review/Order/Claim/Supplier/SourceConfig)
- **Event Bus** (publish/subscribe + idempotency)
- **Search + Facet Index**
- **Trust/Risk Engine**
- **Connector Runtime + Registry**
- **Analytics + Observability**

---

## 3) Architecture blueprint (R4)

### 3.1 Layers (4-level “tree/branch” model)
- **L0 — Runtime/Host:** Android app + (optional) server-mode.
- **L1 — Hub Core:** data model, event bus, indexing, permissions, audit.
- **L2 — Apps:** Compare/Stream/Navigator/Broker/Admin.
- **L3 — Connectors + Bridges:** ingestion/action plugins + external automations.

### 3.2 Data flow (high level)
1) SourceConfig schedules import → Connector fetches data  
2) Connector normalizes → upserts canonical entities/offers/events  
3) Event Bus emits domain events  
4) Indexers update search/facets + graph relations  
5) Apps render views; rules/AI add explanations/summaries  
6) Action connectors handle outbound (affiliate links, webhooks, exports)

### 3.3 Security baseline for R4 platformization
- **Capability sandbox** for connectors:
  - network allowlist, storage constraints, no arbitrary file access
  - explicit PII access permission (default deny)
- **Signed connector packages** + version pinning
- **Contract tests** required to publish a connector to registry
- **Webhook security**: signatures, nonces, replay protection

---

## 4) R4-1: Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges

### 4.1 Connector types
**Ingestion connectors (input):**
- RSS/Atom; Merchant feeds (CSV/TSV/XML); price feeds; review feeds; release notes feeds; partner APIs.

**Action connectors (output):**
- Deeplink generators; outbound webhook; export to CSV/PDF; order routing; partner status updates.

### 4.2 Connector SDK v2 (what’s inside)
- lifecycle: `init → validateConfig → run → emit`
- standard utilities:
  - rate limiting, retries/backoff, ETag caching, timeouts/circuit breaker
  - schema validation on input/output
  - structured logging + ingestion tracing spans
- test harness:
  - golden tests, fuzz tests, contract tests
- governance:
  - versioning, deprecation, migration notes

### 4.3 Internal Marketplace (Registry)
- searchable catalog (by category, source-type, rating, stability)
- install/update/rollback
- compatibility matrix (Hub version ↔ connector version)
- health and reliability score per connector
- license + SBOM + signature metadata

### 4.4 Bridges pack (curated automation)
**Goal:** give “Make-like power” without complexity.
- 10–20 “recipes” v1 (e.g., send Telegram digest, sync to Google Sheets, create Trello card on risk event)
- strict contracts, templates, and observability
- sandbox replay tool for webhooks

### 4.5 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** scalable ecosystem, faster partner onboarding, modular growth.  
**Cons:** requires governance; without contracts you get breakage &amp; chaos.

---

## 5) R4-2: MegaCatalog Navigation (Temu/Ali painkiller)

### 5.1 Key differentiator
A mega-catalog fails when:
- attributes are messy or missing,
- duplicates dominate results,
- filters are weak,
- search doesn’t understand intent.

**Your differentiator:** “Navigator App” builds a *canonical, normalized, deduped* view with hybrid search and guided narrowing.

### 5.2 Subsystems
1) **Normalization engine**
   - units (cm/in, kg/lb), currencies, shipping time formats
   - brand/model dictionaries
   - package/variants (color/storage/bundle)

2) **Entity resolution 2.0**
   - candidate generation (text + attributes + price history + seller)
   - safe merge + rollback
   - graph relations: variant-of, clone-of, alternative, compatible

3) **Hybrid search**
   - lexical (exact for model/MPN/SKU)
   - semantic (meaning, synonyms, typos)
   - facets + explain why-result

4) **Guided search v2**
   - category scripts (questions → facets)
   - store preferences; offer quick toggles

5) **Catalog quality analytics**
   - empty result rate, reformulations, abandon rate
   - attribute completeness, dup ratio
   - “top pain categories” report

6) **(Optional) Visual search**
   - image embeddings for “find similar”
   - risk: compute cost and dataset needs; keep optional behind flag

### 5.3 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** very strong UX, clear UTP vs existing portals.  
**Cons:** more data work; needs careful evaluation to avoid wrong merges.

---

## 6) R4-3: AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label

### 6.1 AI principles (must-have)
- **Evidence-first:** every statement links to hub facts (fields/events/sources).
- **No autonomous buying:** AI suggests; core rules execute.
- **Conservative mode:** if confidence low, ask questions or show alternatives.

### 6.2 Copilot modes
1) **Intent → Query/Facets** (turn natural language into filters)
2) **Explain ranking** (why this offer is top)
3) **Summaries** (events weekly, reviews themes, risk digest)
4) **Action coach** (next best action)
5) **Personalization** (preferences, risk tolerance)
6) **White-label** (tenant config, feature flags, branding)

### 6.3 Personalization and privacy
- opt-in telemetry
- user can view/edit/delete stored preferences
- PII minimization: store preferences, not identities; keep exports safe

### 6.4 White-label packaging
- tenant configs (modules enabled, default lenses, partner lists)
- theme/branding
- rule packs per tenant
- multi-tenant isolation (server-mode) or “profiles” (local mode)

---

## 7) Metrics and success criteria

### 7.1 MegaCatalog success metrics
- ↓ empty-result rate
- ↓ average time-to-first-good-result
- ↓ reformulation count
- ↓ duplicate ratio in top-20 results
- ↑ conversion proxy: clicks to trusted offers / saved shortlist

### 7.2 Stream success metrics
- ↑ daily brief opens
- ↓ notification spam (dedup window hit rate)
- ↑ follow/subscription retention

### 7.3 Connectors platform metrics
- connector install success rate
- ingestion failure rate p95
- MTTR for connector breakage
- registry rollback usage

### 7.4 AI quality &amp; safety metrics
- % answers with evidence links
- hallucination incidents (should be ~0)
- user trust rating per answer (thumbs)
- “AI asked clarifying questions” rate when low confidence

---

## 8) Risks and mitigations
- **Wrong merges** → require moderation queue, rollback, confidence threshold.
- **Connector breakage** (partner changes format) → contract tests + canary + rollback.
- **AI over-claims** → evidence gating + conservative mode + policy templates.
- **Privacy** → PII inventory, opt-in, masking in exports, strict RBAC.
- **Scope creep** → keep curated bridges; avoid “100k integrations” trap.

---

## 9) Roadmap snapshot
- **R4.0:** Connector SDK v2 + Registry v1 + curated Bridges v1 + Hybrid search baseline
- **R4.1:** Normalization &amp; Entity Resolution 2.0 + Guided search v2 + Catalog QA dashboards
- **R4.2:** AI Copilot (intent + summaries) + Personalization controls + White-label beta
- **R4.3:** Optional visual search, advanced risk + multi-tenant hardening

---

## 10) Open questions (to finalize before implementation)
1) Server-mode required from day 1, or “local-first” only with optional server later?
2) Which 10–20 bridges are “must-have” for MVP (Telegram, Sheets, Email, etc.)?
3) Which mega-catalog categories first (electronics? tools? travel offers? insurance tariffs?)?
4) What is the acceptable false-merge rate (target threshold) before auto-merge is allowed?

---

## Appendix A — Terminology
- **Entity:** canonical product/service item
- **Offer:** concrete proposal (price, seller, delivery)
- **Event:** clustered news/price/release/risk update
- **Review:** user review items with topics
- **Trust/Risk:** signals and scores
- **Connector:** plugin for ingest/action
- **Bridge:** curated automation integration
&quot;&quot;&quot;

headers = [&quot;External ID&quot;,&quot;Issue Type&quot;,&quot;Summary&quot;,&quot;Description&quot;,&quot;Acceptance Criteria&quot;,&quot;Priority&quot;,&quot;Story Points&quot;,&quot;Epic Name&quot;,&quot;Epic Link&quot;,&quot;Dependencies&quot;,&quot;Release&quot;,&quot;Estimate T-Shirt&quot;]
rows = [&quot;,&quot;.join([f&quot;\&quot;{h}\&quot;&quot; for h in headers])]

def add_row(ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt):
    row = [ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, str(sp), epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt]
    rows.append(&quot;,&quot;.join([f&quot;\&quot;{str(x).replace(&#x27;\&quot;&#x27;,&#x27;\&quot;\&quot;&#x27;)}\&quot;&quot; for x in row]))

# Epics
add_row(&quot;EPIC-R4-1A&quot;,&quot;Epic&quot;,&quot;R4-1A Connector SDK v2&quot;,&quot;Шаблон/интерфейсы для ingestion/action коннекторов, тестовый harness, стандарты ошибок&quot;,&quot;Новый коннектор создаётся по шаблону и проходит contract tests в CI&quot;,&quot;P0&quot;,8,&quot;R4-1A&quot;,&quot;&quot;,&quot;R1-D09;R1-D08;R1-T27&quot;,&quot;R4&quot;,&quot;L&quot;)

--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
from pathlib import Path

# -----------------------------
# 1) Markdown design document
# -----------------------------
md = &quot;&quot;&quot;# Hub Suite (Compare · Stream · Navigator · Broker) — R4 Product &amp; Technical Design Document
*Version:* 0.9 (Draft)  
*Date:* 2026-01-01  
*Scope:* Roadmap R4 (Connectors/Marketplace/Bridges, MegaCatalog Navigation, AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label)  
*Context:* R1–R3 already cover Hub shell, canonical data model, ingestion basics, search+facets, Stream events, Compare scoring, Orders/Claims, Trust baseline, tech foundation.

---

## 0) Executive summary
You are building a **compact “office-suite style” hub** for commerce &amp; services information:
- **Compare App** — compare offers/services/insurances/travel options with explainable ranking.
- **Stream App** — “news conference” feed: clustered events, price changes, releases, risks, daily/weekly briefs.
- **Navigator App** — solves mega-catalog pain (Temu/Ali): better search, facets, normalization, dedup, guided narrowing.
- **Broker App** — brokerage layer: affiliate/deeplinks, optional order orchestration, service fulfillment routing.

**R4 adds three platform upgrades:**
1) **Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges** (n8n/Node-RED style, but curated and reliable).  
2) **MegaCatalog Navigation** (normalization + entity resolution + hybrid semantic search; optional visual search).  
3) **AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label** (assistant on top; explainability-first; multi-tenant packaging).

---

## 1) Goals and non-goals

### 1.1 Goals (R4)
- Make data acquisition/partners scalable via **connectors** with strict contracts.
- Turn poor mega-catalog experiences into a differentiator: **you find the right item faster**.
- Add AI features that are **safe and evidence-based**: no hallucinated claims, always linked to facts.
- Enable **B2B packaging** (white-label) without creating a fragile mega-monolith.

### 1.2 Non-goals (R4)
- Compete with full Make.com / Zapier ecosystem. Instead: **20–50 curated bridges**.
- “General web crawler” at scale like a search engine. Instead: **source-configured ingestion**.
- Fully automated purchase/payment across all partners. Use **pluggable checkout** and “action connectors”.

---

## 2) Product structure: “Office suite” inside one Hub

### 2.1 Apps (modules) and responsibilities
1) **Compare App**
   - Offer table, sorting, filters, watchlists
   - Scoring + explain panel
   - Export (CSV), share internal links

2) **Stream App**
   - Event clustering (“conference”), timelines
   - Lenses: News, Price, Risk, Release, Reviews
   - Daily/weekly/monthly briefs

3) **Navigator App**
   - Hybrid search + facets
   - Guided narrowing (category wizards)
   - Dedup, canonical entities, normalization
   - “Bad search mode”: typo tolerance, synonym mapping

4) **Broker App**
   - Deeplink/affiliate tracking
   - Optional: order creation + fulfillment routing + claims

5) **Admin/Moderation App**
   - Source Manager, connector install/update
   - Merge queue, risk moderation, compatibility moderation
   - Data quality dashboards

### 2.2 Shared platform services (cross-app)
- **Shared Core Data Model** (Entity/Offer/Event/Review/Order/Claim/Supplier/SourceConfig)
- **Event Bus** (publish/subscribe + idempotency)
- **Search + Facet Index**
- **Trust/Risk Engine**
- **Connector Runtime + Registry**
- **Analytics + Observability**

---

## 3) Architecture blueprint (R4)

### 3.1 Layers (4-level “tree/branch” model)
- **L0 — Runtime/Host:** Android app + (optional) server-mode.
- **L1 — Hub Core:** data model, event bus, indexing, permissions, audit.
- **L2 — Apps:** Compare/Stream/Navigator/Broker/Admin.
- **L3 — Connectors + Bridges:** ingestion/action plugins + external automations.

### 3.2 Data flow (high level)
1) SourceConfig schedules import → Connector fetches data  
2) Connector normalizes → upserts canonical entities/offers/events  
3) Event Bus emits domain events  
4) Indexers update search/facets + graph relations  
5) Apps render views; rules/AI add explanations/summaries  
6) Action connectors handle outbound (affiliate links, webhooks, exports)

### 3.3 Security baseline for R4 platformization
- **Capability sandbox** for connectors:
  - network allowlist, storage constraints, no arbitrary file access
  - explicit PII access permission (default deny)
- **Signed connector packages** + version pinning
- **Contract tests** required to publish a connector to registry
- **Webhook security**: signatures, nonces, replay protection

---

## 4) R4-1: Plugin/Connectors + Marketplace + Bridges

### 4.1 Connector types
**Ingestion connectors (input):**
- RSS/Atom; Merchant feeds (CSV/TSV/XML); price feeds; review feeds; release notes feeds; partner APIs.

**Action connectors (output):**
- Deeplink generators; outbound webhook; export to CSV/PDF; order routing; partner status updates.

### 4.2 Connector SDK v2 (what’s inside)
- lifecycle: `init → validateConfig → run → emit`
- standard utilities:
  - rate limiting, retries/backoff, ETag caching, timeouts/circuit breaker
  - schema validation on input/output
  - structured logging + ingestion tracing spans
- test harness:
  - golden tests, fuzz tests, contract tests
- governance:
  - versioning, deprecation, migration notes

### 4.3 Internal Marketplace (Registry)
- searchable catalog (by category, source-type, rating, stability)
- install/update/rollback
- compatibility matrix (Hub version ↔ connector version)
- health and reliability score per connector
- license + SBOM + signature metadata

### 4.4 Bridges pack (curated automation)
**Goal:** give “Make-like power” without complexity.
- 10–20 “recipes” v1 (e.g., send Telegram digest, sync to Google Sheets, create Trello card on risk event)
- strict contracts, templates, and observability
- sandbox replay tool for webhooks

### 4.5 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** scalable ecosystem, faster partner onboarding, modular growth.  
**Cons:** requires governance; without contracts you get breakage &amp; chaos.

---

## 5) R4-2: MegaCatalog Navigation (Temu/Ali painkiller)

### 5.1 Key differentiator
A mega-catalog fails when:
- attributes are messy or missing,
- duplicates dominate results,
- filters are weak,
- search doesn’t understand intent.

**Your differentiator:** “Navigator App” builds a *canonical, normalized, deduped* view with hybrid search and guided narrowing.

### 5.2 Subsystems
1) **Normalization engine**
   - units (cm/in, kg/lb), currencies, shipping time formats
   - brand/model dictionaries
   - package/variants (color/storage/bundle)

2) **Entity resolution 2.0**
   - candidate generation (text + attributes + price history + seller)
   - safe merge + rollback
   - graph relations: variant-of, clone-of, alternative, compatible

3) **Hybrid search**
   - lexical (exact for model/MPN/SKU)
   - semantic (meaning, synonyms, typos)
   - facets + explain why-result

4) **Guided search v2**
   - category scripts (questions → facets)
   - store preferences; offer quick toggles

5) **Catalog quality analytics**
   - empty result rate, reformulations, abandon rate
   - attribute completeness, dup ratio
   - “top pain categories” report

6) **(Optional) Visual search**
   - image embeddings for “find similar”
   - risk: compute cost and dataset needs; keep optional behind flag

### 5.3 Pros/Cons
**Pros:** very strong UX, clear UTP vs existing portals.  
**Cons:** more data work; needs careful evaluation to avoid wrong merges.

---

## 6) R4-3: AI Copilot + Personalization + White-Label

### 6.1 AI principles (must-have)
- **Evidence-first:** every statement links to hub facts (fields/events/sources).
- **No autonomous buying:** AI suggests; core rules execute.
- **Conservative mode:** if confidence low, ask questions or show alternatives.

### 6.2 Copilot modes
1) **Intent → Query/Facets** (turn natural language into filters)
2) **Explain ranking** (why this offer is top)
3) **Summaries** (events weekly, reviews themes, risk digest)
4) **Action coach** (next best action)
5) **Personalization** (preferences, risk tolerance)
6) **White-label** (tenant config, feature flags, branding)

### 6.3 Personalization and privacy
- opt-in telemetry
- user can view/edit/delete stored preferences
- PII minimization: store preferences, not identities; keep exports safe

### 6.4 White-label packaging
- tenant configs (modules enabled, default lenses, partner lists)
- theme/branding
- rule packs per tenant
- multi-tenant isolation (server-mode) or “profiles” (local mode)

---

## 7) Metrics and success criteria
- MegaCatalog: empty-results ↓, time-to-good-result ↓, duplicate ratio ↓, shortlist saves ↑
- Stream: brief opens ↑, spam ↓, retention ↑
- Platform: ingestion failures ↓, MTTR ↓, rollback safe
- AI: evidence-linked answers ~100%, hallucinations ~0

---

## 8) Roadmap snapshot
- **R4.0:** Connector SDK v2 + Registry v1 + curated Bridges v1 + Hybrid search baseline
- **R4.1:** Normalization &amp; Entity Resolution 2.0 + Guided search v2 + Catalog QA dashboards
- **R4.2:** AI Copilot (intent + summaries) + Personalization controls + White-label beta
- **R4.3:** Optional visual search, advanced risk + multi-tenant hardening
&quot;&quot;&quot;

# -----------------------------
# 2) Backlog CSV (Jira-ready)
# -----------------------------
def q(x):
    s = &quot;&quot; if x is None else str(x)
    return &#x27;&quot;&#x27; + s.replace(&#x27;&quot;&#x27;, &#x27;&quot;&quot;&#x27;) + &#x27;&quot;&#x27;

headers = [
    &quot;External ID&quot;,&quot;Issue Type&quot;,&quot;Summary&quot;,&quot;Description&quot;,&quot;Acceptance Criteria&quot;,&quot;Priority&quot;,
    &quot;Story Points&quot;,&quot;Epic Name&quot;,&quot;Epic Link&quot;,&quot;Dependencies&quot;,&quot;Release&quot;,&quot;Estimate T-Shirt&quot;
]
rows = [&quot;,&quot;.join(q(h) for h in headers)]

def add_row(ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt):
    rows.append(&quot;,&quot;.join(q(v) for v in [
        ext, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, epic_name, epic_link, deps, release, tshirt
    ]))

# Generate stories for all epics
for key, *_ in epics:
    templates = story_templates.get(key, [])
    for suffix, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, tshirt, dep_suffix in templates:
        ext_id = f&quot;{key}{suffix}&quot;
        deps = f&quot;{key}{dep_suffix}&quot; if dep_suffix else &quot;&quot;
        add_row(ext_id, itype, summary, desc, ac, prio, sp, &quot;&quot;, f&quot;EPIC-{key}&quot;, deps, &quot;R4&quot;, tshirt)

out_dir = Path(&quot;/mnt/data&quot;)
md_path = out_dir / &quot;hub_r4_design_doc.md&quot;
csv_path = out_dir / &quot;hub_r4_backlog.csv&quot;
md_path.write_text(md, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;)
csv_path.write_text(&quot;\n&quot;.join(rows), encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;)

(len(rows)-1, md_path.as_posix(), csv_path.as_posix())

## Анализ “самого начала чата” и что уже превращено в пары (до 4)
В начале вы задали **4 больших ключевых понятия**:

1) **Портал сравнения** (товары/услуги/страховки/путешествия)  
2) **Новостная лента / “новостная конференция”** (сравнение событий/новостей/выходов/отзывов)  
3) **Дропшиппинг/посредник** (не только товары, но и цифровые товары/услуги)  
4) **Китайские мегакаталоги с плохой навигацией** (поиск/фильтры/краулинг как отдельная “машина поиска”)

Эти 4 смысла у нас сейчас закрыты **первой четверкой пар**:

- **R5 (MD+CSV):** источники/партнёрки/API + каталог коннекторов (для “входа данных”)  
- **R6 (MD+CSV):** каноническая модель данных + data dictionary (чтобы модули “говорили” одним языком)  
- **R7 (MD+CSV):** blueprint “набор приложений как Office” + матрица модуль-функции (как это собрать в suite)  
- **R8 (MD+CSV):** комплаенс/антифрод/модерация + risk register (чтобы это было жизнеспособно в реальности)

--- ПОЛЬЗОВАТЕЛЬ ---
Сколько ещё R

--- АССИСТЕНТ ---
Сейчас у нас сделано **до R144** включительно.

**Сколько ещё будет R — заранее фиксированного “потолка” нет.** Это серия, которую можно продолжать столько, сколько нужно под ваш “пакет” (как офисный suite: можно 10 модулей, можно 100).

Чтобы было понятно “сколько осталось”, можно считать от выбранной цели:

- цель **R150** → осталось **6** (R145–R150)  
- цель **R160** → осталось **16**  
- цель **R180** → осталось **36**  
- цель **R200** → осталось **56**

Если ориентироваться на практичный “Suite v1” (закрыть роли/права, публичные страницы/SEO, финальную упаковку/индекс/релизные артефакты), то обычно достаточно **примерно до R150–R160**.
